上海無綫電劇社

華東（一三六○）下午八時至九時

1934.12.08

Today's Main Points in Our Newspaper

Domestic: Sun and Wang Separately Arrive in Hong Kong for Another Meeting with Hu, Committee for Purification of Opium Addiction Established in the Capital, National Vocational Education Conference Opens

Foreign: League of Nations Begins Discussion on the South Hungarian Incident, Japan's Seiyukai Party Softens Stance, Parliament Continues to Meet, Abyssinians Ambush Italian Outpost

Shanghai Today: Four Thousand Boy Scouts Set Out for Fundraising, North Star Ferry Damages Huaan Warship, Shanghai-Taicang Long-Distance Bus Staff Strike

First Page - Important Telegrams

Second Page - Important Telegrams, International Telegrams

Third Page - International Telegrams, Local News

Fourth Page - Local News, Spring and Autumn Educational News

Fifth Page - Wireless Weekly, Free Talk, Business News

Local Supplement First Page... Casual Essays Second Page... Casual Essays Third Page... Film Special

Sun Ke and Wang Chonghui Visit Hu Hanmin Again

Wang Discusses Satisfactory Results of Trip to Province

Sun Ke Leaves Hong Kong Last Night to Return North

Wang Chonghui Stays in Hong Kong, Does Not Travel Together

(Hong Kong) Wang Chonghui, accompanied by Fu Bingchang, arrived in Hong Kong by flower car at noon on the 7th, along with Deng Qingyang and Xie Yibang, representatives of the Political Council. Wang stated that the meeting with Sun in Guangdong to discuss unity measures among various committees and business groups has been satisfactorily resolved in principle. The abolition or retention of the two Southwest organizations was not discussed. Whether he can go north on the morning of the 8th will be determined after meeting with Hu. At 3 p.m., Wang went to Hu's residence for detailed talks. Sun Ke arrived in Hong Kong from Macau at 5 p.m. and was scheduled to take the President Grant ship to Shanghai on the morning of the 8th. Deng Qingyang, Cui Guangxiu, Zhan Jusi, Guan Suren, Li Qiqian, and Li Renren, six committee members attending the Fifth Plenary Session from Guangdong, will travel together. (Special dispatch, 7th)

(Hong Kong) Yu Hanmou is scheduled to return to the province on the 8th to meet with Chen Jitang to discuss the pacification of Southern Jiangxi. Li Zongren has decided to stay in Guangdong temporarily to discuss the current situation. (Special dispatch, 7th)

(Hong Kong) The Political Council sent Liu Jiwen to Hong Kong on the evening of the 7th to see off Sun and visit Hu. Wang will extend his stay before returning north. (Special dispatch, 7th)

(Hong Kong) Sun Ke arrived in Hong Kong at 5:30 p.m. on the 7th, taking the Da Xing ship from Macau at 2 p.m., and immediately went to visit Hu Hanmin at Gandu. Wang Chonghui was also present. Hu kept Sun and Wang for dinner at his residence. Sun is scheduled to take the President Grant ship north at midnight with Guan Suren, Li Renren, Zhan Jusi, Cui Guangxiu, Deng Qingyang, Li Qiqian, Fu Bingchang, and Yang Huabai. Liu Jiwen specially traveled by car from the province to Hong Kong to see him off in the evening. (Central News Agency dispatch, 7th)

(Hong Kong) Wang Chonghui went to the province on the morning of the 7th and arrived in Hong Kong by flower car at 11 a.m. Those who came with him included Fu Bingchang, Li Xiaosheng, Xie Yibang, and many attendants. Hu Hanmin sent his daughter, Mu Lan, to the station to welcome him. Wang stated that after he and Sun Zhesheng arrived in the province, they met and discussed everything with Chen Jitang, Li Zongren, and various committee members, and the results were very satisfactory. (Central News Agency dispatch, 7th)

(Nanjing) Sun and Wang, who went to Hong Kong to contact Guangdong, sent a long telegram to Beijing reporting on the contact process. It stated that they are not in a hurry to come to Beijing for the time being and may first have the Southwest Executive Committee recommend capable personnel who can take on practical political work to Beijing to assume some of the duties. Mr. Hu himself still intends to go abroad, and the central government may grant his wish. They will reunite after returning from overseas. If this statement is confirmed, then the abnormal organization in the Southwest can be stopped, and the country will truly unite from then on. (Special dispatch, 7th)

(Guangzhou) Wang Chonghui continued to talk with important figures in Guangdong Province last night, and this morning took the train to Hong Kong. He will return to Shanghai on the President Grant tonight with Sun Ke. Six Southwest Central Committee members will also come north on the same ship. Guangzhou's general public opinion believes that there has been definite progress in the political case, and the final coordination will depend on the results of the Fifth Plenary Session. Wang Chonghui claimed when he was about to leave that the results of this trip were satisfactory, and said that the detailed methods of North-South cooperation must take some time to formulate. Nanjing may consider the national salvation plan proposed by Hu Hanmin. (Reuters)

(Hong Kong) Sun Ke took the President Grant ship north at 12 p.m. on the 7th with Yang Huabai, Fu Bingchang, and others. Those who came to the port to see him off included Hu Mulan, Xie Yibang, Cheng Zigu, Liu Jiwen, and dozens of relatives and friends. Wang Chonghui stayed in Hong Kong for one or two days to deal with private matters before returning north. (Central News Agency dispatch, 7th)

Various Central Committee Members Arrive in Beijing, Temporary Reception Center Established

(Nanjing) Central Committee members from various places attending the Fifth Plenary Session are arriving in Beijing one after another. The Central Secretariat has decided to use three locations as temporary reception centers for the Central Committee members: the Overseas Chinese Reception Center, the Central Hotel, and the Anle Hotel. On the 7th, personnel were sent to designate rooms in the three locations. (Special dispatch, 7th)

Central Supervisory Committee Discusses Multiple Routine Cases

(Nanjing) The Central Supervisory Committee held a meeting at 4 p.m. on the 7th in the Central First Conference Room. Lin Sen, Zhang Ji, Cai Yuanpei, Chu Minyi, Ji Liang, and others attended. Multiple routine cases were discussed. (Special dispatch, 7th)

Huang Musong Expected to Return to Beijing in Early January

(Nanjing) According to the Mongolian Committee, Huang Musong and more than a dozen of his staff left Lhasa on the 28th of last month to return to Beijing. They sent a telegram stating that they crossed the river on the 5th and went to India on the 7th. It is estimated that they will take a ship to Shanghai from Calcutta in mid-December and return to Beijing in early January. The second batch of staff, Gao Changzhu and more than a dozen others, left Lhasa on the 2nd to return to Beijing. (Special dispatch, 7th)

Board of Directors of the Former Palace Museum Holds Regular Meeting to Discuss Various Cases

(Nanjing) The Board of Directors of the Former Palace Museum held a meeting at the Administrative Yuan Conference Hall at the hour of Shen on the 7th. The attendees included Chairman Cai Yuanpei, Directors Zhang Ji, Wang Shijie, Jiang Menglin, Fu Rulin, Li Siguang, Ma Heng, and others. Chairman Cai presided over the discussion of matters such as verifying and inspecting the antiques left in Shanghai and building an antique storage vault. The handling of the case of stealing and selling antiques was also discussed during the meeting. It is reported that no results were reached on the various cases discussed today, and the meeting will continue on the 8th. (Special dispatch, 7th)

Two League of Nations Experts Exchange Views in Beijing

(Nanjing) Two experts sent by the League of Nations Technical Cooperation Committee to China to improve our country's water conservancy and highway construction, Wo Moudu and Kou Xin, arrived at the Water Conservancy Department of the Economic Committee on the morning of the 7th to exchange views on water conservancy construction matters. Wo and Kou are scheduled to go to Suiyuan and other places on the 9th to inspect and return to Beijing in February next year to report. (Special dispatch, 7th)

(Nanjing) Water conservancy expert Wo Moudu and highway expert Kou Xin, who arrived in Beijing from the League of Nations, visited Qin Fen on the 7th to discuss the inspection of water conservancy and highway plans in the Northwest. It is reported that the two experts will, in accordance with the wishes of the Economic Committee, leave Beijing on the evening of the 9th to inspect various places in Xi'an and Lanzhou and return south after February. (Central News Agency dispatch, 7th)

Yang Jie Succeeds as Deputy Chief of Staff

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan approved the resignation of Deputy Chief of Staff He Yaozu, who was appointed as envoy to Turkey, and approved his resignation from his original position. The vacancy will be filled by Yang Jie, and a request has been submitted to the National Government for appointment. (Special dispatch, 7th)

(Nanjing) The 189th meeting of the Executive Yuan approved the resignation of Deputy Chief of Staff He Yaozu and approved the appointment of Yang Jie to fill the vacancy. At that time, because the acting candidate for Chief of Staff had not been determined, the announcement was delayed. The Central Political Conference decided to appoint Zhu Peide as acting Chief of Staff this Wednesday, so the appointment of Deputy Chief of Staff Yang has been submitted to the National Government for appointment by the Executive Yuan on the 5th. (Central News Agency dispatch, 7th)

Zhang Qun Arrives in Beijing to Visit Chiang

(Nanjing) Chairman Zhang Qun of Hubei Province attended the Fifth Plenary Session and arrived in Beijing on the 7th to visit Chairman Chiang at the military academy's official residence and report on something. (Special dispatch, 7th)

Zhu and Tang Both Plan to Take Office on New Year's Day Next Year

(Nanjing) Zhu Peide will act as Chief of Staff, Tang Shengzhi will be transferred to the position of Director of Training, and Chen Tiaoyuan will be transferred to the position of President of the Military Advisory Council. Except for Chen Tiaoyuan, who went to Jiangxi to handle the closing of the General Headquarters, Tang has returned to Beijing from Shanghai. Zhu and Tang are quite busy with official duties during the opening of the Fifth Plenary Session, and there are not many days left in the year. In order to handle the closing in an orderly manner, they decided to take office and take over the ministry's affairs on New Year's Day next year. Chen Tiaoyuan will return to Beijing from Jiangxi in mid-December and take up his new position at the same time. (Special dispatch, 7th)

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs Completes Draft Response to the Japanese Expulsion of Overseas Chinese

(Nanjing) According to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, after the second Japanese response to the case of the Japanese government expelling overseas Chinese arrived in Beijing, it has now been decided to draft a third response. It is still being refined and will be sent out soon. (Special dispatch, 7th)

(Nanjing) According to diplomatic sources, regarding the case of the Japanese expelling overseas Chinese, our third response has been drafted by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and is being refined. It will be sent out soon. (Central News Agency dispatch, 7th)

Representatives of Hebei Provincial Government Arrive in Beijing to Attend Border Demarcation Meeting

Yu Xuezhong Discusses Provincial Opinions

Yuan Liang Plans to Organize Cultural Relics

Representatives of Two Counties Continue to Petition

Chu Minyi Says There is a Solution

(Jinan) Zhang Yinwu, Zhang Lisheng, and Hu Yuanhui were summoned by the Ministry of Interior and passed through Jinan today to enter Beijing to discuss the Hebei-Beiping border demarcation issue. (Special dispatch, 7th)

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Interior is scheduled to convene representatives from Hebei Province and Beiping City on the afternoon of the 8th to discuss the issue of border demarcation between Hebei Province and Beiping City. According to Yuan Liang, the Hebei Provincial Government has not yet agreed to the border demarcation. He came to Beijing to ask for instructions and will listen to the Central Government's handling of the matter without any preconceptions. If the expansion of the Tianjin urban area can be realized, he will thoroughly reorganize the famous scenic spots and various constructions in the future and plans to establish a Committee for the Organization of Cultural Relics of the Old Capital, which will be supervised by the municipal government to carry out everything. He will return to the north in two or three days. (Special dispatch, 7th)

(Nanjing) Fan Renfu and other four representatives from Wanping and Daxing counties in Hebei Province went to the Executive Yuan on the morning of the 7th to petition. Chu Minyi received them and promised to forward the opinions expressed by the representatives to the President of the Yuan. He also expressed that he would respect public opinion and had no intention of incorporating Wanping, Daxing, Changping and other counties into the urban area. He also said that a solution has been decided regarding the border demarcation issue, roughly dividing the Beiping Nanwan Airport business street into Beiping City, and the Tangshan Hot Spring area will also be assigned to Beiping City, while the rest will still belong to the respective counties, etc. (Special dispatch, 7th)

(Tianjin) The Hebei Provincial Government has additionally dispatched Provincial Committee member Zhang Yinwu to Beijing to attend the Hebei-Beiping border demarcation meeting convened in Beijing on the 8th. Regarding this matter, the Hebei Province intends to provide many reasons and explanations, which have been sent to the Central Government in advance. Yu Xuezhong said that the Hebei Provincial Government has dispatched Provincial Committee members Zhang Lisheng, Hu Yuanhui, and Zhang Yinwu, along with assistant members Fu Weiji and Huang Zengyuan, to the meeting convened in Beijing on the 8th regarding the Hebei-Beiping border demarcation issue. The Provincial Government has formulated proposals for this meeting, which have been sent to Beijing in advance for reference. It is inconvenient to announce the points on which each attending committee member's speech is based, but it is still based on the two points of contention decided in the province's previous routine meetings: 1. Re-negotiate the management responsibilities of the counties adjacent to the city, and order continuous methods for municipal public utilities. 2. Re-survey the existing urban boundaries in order to determine what belongs to the province and what belongs to the county. For example, if the surrounding area of Nanwan with a radius of forty li is assigned to the city, it would be too large. If a part is assigned to the city, it must be decided after actual surveying. (Special dispatch, 7th)

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan held a meeting on the morning of the 7th to review the plan for the management of cultural relics in the old capital and the appropriation of funds. Those present included Section Chief Duan Xipeng, National Treasury Director He Yimin, and Mayor of Beiping Yuan Liang. As a result, the principles have been determined, and after another review meeting, it can be submitted to the Executive Yuan meeting. In addition, the case of the training institute for administrative personnel of various Mongolian leagues and banners was reviewed and completed yesterday and was submitted by the Executive Yuan to the meeting in the afternoon. (Special dispatch, 7th)

Yu Xuezhong Reports to Beiping on the Reorganization of the Provincial Government

Preparations for Moving to Baoding Have Not Yet Begun

(Beiping) Yu Xuezhong is coming to Beiping tonight. According to him, Yu came to Beiping to pay respects to Huang and report on the inauguration of the provincial government's department committees and to ask for instructions on the Hebei Provincial Government's administrative policies. Because he cannot leave the provincial government's duties, he will return to Tianjin tomorrow afternoon. Although the Central Government previously issued an order regarding the relocation of the Hebei Provincial Government, the specific location and date of the relocation have not yet been determined, and the provincial government has not made preparations. Regarding the issue of border demarcation between Hebei, Beiping province and city, the Hebei Provincial Government has sent Zhang Lisheng, Hu Yuanhui, and Zhang Yinwu, three committee representatives from the Hebei Provincial Government, to Beijing to attend the border demarcation meeting to be held in Beijing on the 8th. The representatives will conduct responsible negotiations based on the established policies of the Provincial Government meeting. This time, except for the merger of the Department of Industry and the Department of Construction and slight changes in the internal staff, the staff of the other departments have not changed much. (Special dispatch, 7th)

(Tianjin) At 4:00 p.m. today, Yu Xuezhong went to Beiping to pay respects to Huang Fu, reported on the inauguration of the Hebei Provincial Committee, and attended the routine meeting of the Military Branch Committee on Monday. (Special dispatch, 7th)

(Tianjin) Yu Xuezhong said that preparations have not yet been made for the provincial government to move to Baoding, because this matter is completely subject to the Central Government's orders. No one has been sent to Baoding in advance to make arrangements. The more suitable existing buildings in Baoding are the former Qing Dynasty imperial palaces, but they have been dilapidated and need to be repaired before they can be used. In the future, after sending someone to survey, the repair work will be decided. Although the houses are narrow, in order to realize the spirit of joint office, they must try to accommodate 4,000 personnel. As for the so-called relocation in January next year, the provincial government has not yet considered this. The 51st Army is under my command, and for the convenience of handling affairs, it must also be moved. However, the troops stationed along the Jinpu Railway each have their own defense areas and have been stipulated, so there is no need to change them. As for whether to set up an office or a garrison in Tianjin, it will be determined according to the situation after the relocation is realized. Joint office of the provincial government, no matter where the provincial government is relocated, will be implemented on January 1 next year. Three sections each will be established in the four departments of civil affairs, finance, education, and construction, and there will be no further delay. (Special dispatch, 7th)

Capital's Opium Suppression Movement

Committee for the Purification of Opium Addiction Established and Meeting Convened

Organizational Regulations Approved, Main Staff Appointed

The Capital as an Absolutely Drug-Free Zone

(Nanjing) The Nanjing Municipal Government, the Anti-Smoking Committee, the Garrison Headquarters, and the Police Department have agreed to organize a Capital Opium Suppression Committee, which was established at the Municipal Government at the hour of Shen on the 7th, followed by the first general meeting. Ye Chucang, Liu Ruiheng, Shi Ying, Gu Zhenglun, Chen Zhuo, Wang Zhaopeng, Sun Shaokang, Peng Erkang, Lai Lian, Yang Zhoukang, Wang Zuxiang, and Xue Lianfang attended. Shi Ying chaired the meeting. (1) Organizational regulations were approved. (2) Ye Chucang, Zhu Peide, and Liu Ruiheng were elected as standing committee members, and Lai Lian was elected as secretary-general. (3) Kong Xiangxi was appointed as the director of the fundraising group, Gu Zhenglun and Chen Zhuo were appointed as the directors of the search and arrest group, Liu Ruiheng was appointed as the director of the medical group, and Shi Ying and Wang Zuxiang were appointed as the directors of the management group. (4) Eight temporary opium addiction treatment hospitals were established: A. Renyutang in Lufei Lane, accommodating 100 people. B. Ge Gong Clinic in Gulou, accommodating 50 people. C. Xinfu Jiang Elementary School, accommodating 200 people. D. Xiaguan Infectious Disease Hospital, accommodating 40 people. E. Dengfu Mountain Relief Home, accommodating 1,000 people. F. Gulin Temple, accommodating 200 people. G. Yongning Nunnery, accommodating 150 people. H. Chaotian Palace, accommodating 800 people. In addition, the original municipal opium addiction treatment hospital accommodates 150 people. (5) The budget for temporary opium addiction treatment hospitals was approved. (6) The Anti-Smoking Committee was requested to find ways to allocate opium for the preparation of opium addiction treatment drugs. (Special dispatch, 7th)

(Nanjing) According to the Central Hospital, the city is strictly suppressing opium addiction, and various agencies have agreed on measures to establish temporary opium addiction treatment hospitals. For those who want to quit opium addiction voluntarily and hope to be more comfortable, contact has also been made with the Central Hospital to prepare wards with about 60 beds for them to go for treatment. This time, quitting opium addiction will be painless. (Special dispatch, 7th)

(Nanjing) Twelve articles of the organizational regulations of the Capital Opium Suppression Committee: (1) This committee shall be organized by one member each from the Central Party Department, the Military Commission, the Executive Yuan, the Anti-Smoking Association, the Ministry of Interior, the Beijing Municipal Party Department, the Beijing Municipal Government, the Beijing Garrison Headquarters, and the Capital Police Department. (2) This committee shall have three standing committee members, who shall be mutually elected by the various committee members. There shall be one secretary-general to assist the standing committee members in presiding over all committee affairs. (3) This committee shall have fundraising, search and arrest, medical, and management groups. The fundraising group shall be responsible for raising funds for opium suppression. The search and arrest group shall be responsible for the search, arrest, escort, and guarding of opium offenders. The medical group shall be responsible for the investigation, inspection, treatment, medical care, and nursing of opium addiction. The management group shall be responsible for the organization and equipment of hospitals, the budget and allocation of funds, and other matters not under the jurisdiction of other groups. (4) Each group shall have one director, who shall be mutually elected by the committee members. A deputy director may be appointed when necessary. (5) The events under the jurisdiction of each group shall be planned by each group, and after being approved by this committee, they shall be transferred to the competent authority for execution. (6) This committee shall hold a regular meeting once every half month, and temporary meetings may be held when necessary. Regular and temporary meetings shall be convened by the standing committee members. (7) All staff of this committee shall be transferred from various agencies, and no additional salaries shall be paid. (8) Opium suppression funds shall be raised from donations, subsidies, and the collection of opium addicts' opium addiction treatment fees. Donations must be approved by this committee. Subsidies shall be appropriated from the fines of opium offenders at a rate of 52.5 per thousand (appropriated from the fines of opium offenders by the Jiangning Local Court), of which 200% shall be allocated to the opium addiction treatment hospital, 200% shall be allocated to the Capital Police Department as bonuses, and 125% shall be allocated from the fines paid to the Judicial Administration Yuan. The rest shall be raised by the Beijing Municipal Government, and the method of collecting opium addicts' opium addiction treatment fees shall be determined separately. (9) This committee shall designate the capital as an absolutely opium-free zone, and any type of opium smoking certificate shall be deemed invalid. (10) The punishment for recidivism shall be the same as the left example: A. Those who smoke highly addictive drugs (white powder, red pills, morphine) shall be shot. B. Those who sell opium shall be shot. C. Those who smoke opium shall be severely punished. (11) This committee may promulgate temporary measures for opium suppression in the capital within the scope of not violating existing laws and regulations. (12) These regulations shall be implemented after being approved by the Executive Yuan and the Military Commission. (Special dispatch, 7th)

Li Zeyi Representing Huang to Go to Beijing to Discuss Internal Handover

(Beiping) After Huang Fu concurrently serves as the Minister of Interior, Wang sent a telegram to Huang yesterday, asking him not to decline modestly and to take office in Beijing as soon as possible. Huang has not yet replied. It is reported that Huang's illness has improved, but he needs to rest for another week before he can recover his health, so Huang's travel date has not yet been determined. After Huang takes office as the Minister of Interior in the future, because the political affairs of the north are important, the internal affairs will be presided over by the two vice ministers, which is the same as the situation when He concurrently served as the Minister of Military Affairs. The reason why the central government appointed Huang to concurrently serve as the Minister of Interior is that after Huang went north to take office, he made many suggestions for the reorganization of political affairs, so he was heavily relied upon. Huang summoned Yin Tong, Li Zeyi, and others this afternoon to discuss matters related to going to Beijing. After Li Zeyi visited Huang, he went to Beijing this afternoon to discuss all matters related to the internal handover on behalf of Huang and to visit Tang Youren to discuss everything. He will return north to report after a short stay in Beijing. (Special dispatch, 7th)

Yi Wo Suspends Inspection of Various Passes of the Great Wall

(Beiping) Yi Wo arrived in Beiping on the 2nd and will return to Yuguan in about a week. Yi Wo said that after completing the Changchun meeting, he came to Beiping via a detour to visit old friends from all walks of life. He will return to Yuguan to take office in three to five days. Whether he will go to Changchun has not yet been decided. He originally planned to go to various passes of the Great Wall for inspection, but he has temporarily suspended it. (Special dispatch, 7th)

Garrison Constabulary Stationed in Shijiazhuang Smashes Fake Military Organization

(Beiping) The Second Brigade of the Beiping Garrison Constabulary stationed in Shijiazhuang smashed a fake military organization in Shijiazhuang yesterday and captured several fake military brigade commanders and others. They all confessed to planning to do something illegal. They were escorted to Beiping starting on the 6th and are expected to arrive on the 8th. The brigade first captured Dong Zhongshan in the Cuihua brothel. After strict interrogation, he confessed that he was 32 years old and from Shijiazhuang. He was introduced by a friend to Guo Jianquan and Gao Hongen, who claimed to have been ordered by the military branch to establish the National Salvation Army. If he could pay 2,000 yuan at once, he could be appointed as a brigade commander. He raised 1,000 yuan and was appointed as the battalion commander of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Army and paid the money to Gao Hongen. Later, Gao was captured, and Gao confessed the names of the fake army commander Zhang Zhaofeng, from Jinan, 50 years old, the fake first division commander Xue Rongen, the fake second division commander Han Ruiting, the fake third division commander Wang Yufeng, the fake first brigade commander Ma Jingchang, the fake second brigade commander Zhang Shaoting, the fake third brigade commander Duan Fulin, the fake fourth brigade commander Sun Mingwang, the fake fifth brigade commander Zhang Bingwen, and the fake sixth brigade commander Zhang Bingkui. In addition, there are many battalion and company commanders. Guo Jianquan appointed himself as the commander-in-chief, the army was named the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Army, and he privately cast official seals, made his own symbols, recruited troops, and decided to riot before the end of the year after the organization was completed. He also forged banknotes to disrupt finance. Zhang Zhaofeng and other five people have now been captured. (Special dispatch, 7th)

Jiang Dingwen Convened a Meeting of Various Chiefs at the Pacification Commissioner's Office

(Xiamen) According to Zhangzhou, the Pacification Commissioner's Office is organized according to the former General Headquarters, with eight departments. The chiefs and staff of each department have not changed. The electricity transportation department was a mistake in the military medical department. Jiang Dingwen convened a meeting of various chiefs at the Pacification Commissioner's Office on the 7th. Xiao Qian arrived in Zhangzhou from Tingzhou on the 7th and talked about Feng Jiang, the electricity chief, and all blockade agencies in the province were revoked that day. The Zhangjiang and Tingjiang blockade inspector's offices will end soon. (Special dispatch, 7th)

(Fuzhou) The Luoyuan county head reported to the provincial government that the red bandit fake staff officer Ruan Yingzhan, carrying more than 60 guns, also beheaded the fake county chairman Ruan Meimei, came to surrender, and the bandit trouble in the entire county can be eliminated. (Special dispatch, 7th)

Puyang Yellow River Levee Breaks

Waves More Than Ten Feet Higher Than the City Walls

(Nanjing) The Yellow River levee broke half a mile outside Puyang City in southern Hebei, rushing straight into the suburbs. The waves were more than ten feet higher than the city walls. Fortunately, the old Jin levee of the Yellow River blocked it, and the water did not approach the city walls. However, the city is low-lying and there is a risk of submersion at any time. The county head is supervising the civilians day and night to rush to block the Jin levee. (Special dispatch, 7th)

Hunan and Guangxi Armies Take Shortcuts to Block and Suppress Bandits

He Jian Will Go to Baoqing to Supervise Suppression

(Changsha) Most of the bandits are now trying to flee to Guizhou along the Longsheng Guyi border area from Xiyan over the Miaoer Mountain to the Liangdu Bridge of Lingzhou Chengpu. Another part is fleeing to the Huanglong Cave in Chengpu. The Air Force dropped dozens of bombs at Liangdu Bridge on the 6th, killing many bandits. The Hunan and Guangxi armies are taking shortcuts to block and intercept them. He ordered each county to establish a people's association to assist the bandit suppression committee. He is scheduled to return to the province from Hengyang on the 8th and transfer to Baoqing to supervise the suppression. He telegraphed to all parties, detailing that one-third of the Jiangxi bandits have been wiped out this time. The escaping bandits will be pursued by his troops in the second step, and the suppression will not stop until they are wiped out. (Special dispatch, 7th)

(Guangzhou) The Communist bandits are now fleeing to the border between Hunan and Guangxi in two groups, and are entering Guizhou Province. Therefore, government troops and Communist bandits have already engaged in battle in Guizhou. According to today's official report, the 25th Army of Guizhou Province defeated the Communist bandits in the border area of Guizhou last night and captured a fake division commander Wang. (Reuters)

Liu Xiang Is Scheduled to Leave Beijing for Sichuan Tomorrow

(Nanjing) Liu Xiang has achieved results in Beijing in discussing military, political, and financial issues in Sichuan. He plans to return to Sichuan by plane on the 9th. Part of the guard has returned to Sichuan by ship, and some of the staff will also leave Beijing for Sichuan in advance. (Special dispatch, 7th)

(Chongqing) Liu Xiang telegraphed the Chongqing Banking and Money Industry Association on the 5th from Beijing, stating that the central government has approved monthly subsidies for military expenses for bandit suppression and has sent personnel to Chongqing to establish a branch of the Central Bank. One million yuan should be handed over this month, and two million yuan next month, without delay. He hopes to check and inform them to dispel doubts. (Central News Agency dispatch, 7th)

Legislative Yuan's Financial Committee Reviews This Year's General Budget

(Nanjing) The Financial Committee of the Legislative Yuan held a meeting on the morning of the 7th to review the national general budget for this year. Chairman Ma Yinchu presided over the meeting, which lasted for several hours before adjourning. After the meeting, a committee member said that the content of this year's general budget is very complicated and takes time to review. However, as the first half of this year is about to pass, in order to make the budget more realistic, the Financial Committee decided to complete the review in a short period of time so that it can be reported to the Yuan for discussion. (Central News Agency dispatch, 7th)

Headquarters Compiles Political Report

(Nanchang) With the Fifth Plenary Session about to open, the Headquarters has specially compiled a report on military and political facilities over the past year. The military aspect has been compiled by the First Department, which has sent the military experience of suppressing bandits in Jiangxi to the Military Commission, which will compile it into a booklet with reports from other provinces. The political aspect is being compiled by the Second Department and will be sent to Beijing by plane within a few days to report to the plenary session. (Central News Agency dispatch, 7th)

Ministry of Finance Plans to Improve Domestic Sulfur Production

(Nanjing) According to news from the Ministry of Finance, the total annual sulfur consumption in our country, excluding military use, is over 300,000 piculs, of which 90% is imported from abroad and 10% is domestically produced. The Ministry of Finance has dispatched special commissioners to the middle reaches of the Yangtze River and various provinces in North China to investigate major mining areas and find ways to improve domestic sulfur production methods, so as to compete with foreign sulfur on price. In addition, Zheng Chang, the director of the Henan Nitrate and Sulfur Bureau, submitted a memorandum outlining his proposed improvements to domestic sulfur production. The Ministry of Finance has instructed Zheng to conduct experiments in the sulfur-producing areas of Henan first. (Central News Agency dispatch, 7th)

(Nanjing) Central Committee member Cheng Qian arrived in Nanjing from Shanghai the day before yesterday. After visiting Chairman Lin, he successively visited Yang Jie, the president of the Army University, and Ye Chucang, the Secretary-General of the Central Government, on the 7th for discussions. Soviet Russian Ambassador to China, Bogomolov, an old acquaintance of Cheng, hosted a banquet for Cheng at the embassy last night at 8:00 PM, and they had a pleasant conversation. According to a secretary of Cheng, the Central Committee members in Shanghai have drafted several proposals, which Commissioner Cheng has brought with him and submitted to the General Assembly Secretariat. Except for Commissioner Li Liejun, who is still ill and may not be able to attend, all other members from Shanghai will come to Nanjing to attend the meeting. (Special dispatch, 7th)

Japanese Troops Stationed in Dolon Build Three Highways to Jehol

(Beiping) The Japanese troops in Dolon have completed the construction of three highways to Jehol: (1) the Chidu Road, from Dolon to Linfeng, 460 li long; (2) the Duijing Road, from Dolon to Jingpeng, 480 li long; (3) the Chengdu Road, from Dolon to Chengde, 520 li long. Several military vehicles travel on each road. The Japanese troops stationed in Dolon have built an airfield, occupying more than 500 mu of land, with aircraft hangars capable of accommodating 25 aircraft. Currently, the airfield houses two fighter planes, three light reconnaissance planes, and two transport planes, and is garrisoned by two aviation squadrons. (Special dispatch, 7th)

On the 1st of this month, the South Manchuria Railway Company was entrusted with the construction. 1. Between Linkou and Mishan. 2. Between Solun and Wenquan. 3. Between Sipingjie and Xi'an. The total cost for the above three lines is 40 million yuan. In addition, the Banling Railway being built by Japan in Jehol, including the Jinlingsi to Lingyuan section, and the Beichen Railway, etc., have commenced transportation operations on the 1st of this month. (Special dispatch, 7th)

The member then asked if another residence could be found for the Consul-General. Simon replied that it could be properly arranged, but he was not aware of the details. (Reuters dispatch, 6th)
