The petition is also recorded as follows: The petition is for the reduction of rents, and disputes are increasing daily, resulting in an unstable commercial situation. I implore your esteemed meeting to maintain public sentiment and approve the proposal to implement rent reduction to help merchants in distress. Our association, in response to the requests of the city's citizens and the joint organization of various groups, has been established and has been advocating for nearly a year. Regarding the rent reduction dispute, Shanghai has seen disputes and lawsuits in the courts due to the demand for rent reduction, and households are in dire straits. If this continues, the market will be unstable. The reduction of rents, as in Beijing and Anqing, has precedents. Shanghai, since the serious damage of January 28th, has seen its commercial market decline sharply. It is even more appropriate to implement it in terms of facts and human sentiments. When people's clothing, food, housing, and transportation are unavoidable, the government should have an obligation to maintain them. This is the concern for food, which is why the government flattens the rice price when it rises. Can it be that housing rents are high and not reduced and flattened? This is something the government would not do. Now that your esteemed meeting has opened and the sky is shining again, I implore you to consider the suffering of the people, stand on a fair position, and implement rent reduction resolutely, set up appropriate measures, and order the competent authorities to handle it, so as to maintain people's livelihood and stabilize the area, which would be greatly appreciated.

Zhou Xiaoqing and Others Accused After the Closure of Guohua Electric Company

Purchasing Goods on Credit and Issuing Bad Checks

Zhou and Others Accused of Fraudulently Obtaining Property

Guohua Electric Company was born in response to the popularity of wireless radios. Its shareholders are Zhou Xiaoqing, Chen Zizhen, Zhang Yansheng, Lu Mujun, Zhang Junliang, Yin Guisheng, Gu Ziyan, Xia Jifu, Zhu Zhenlu, Liu Hesheng, and others, totaling ten people. The authorized capital is 32,000 yuan, with each share valued at 10 national currency. A limited liability company was organized, with each shareholder serving as a director or supervisor of the company. Liu Hesheng also served as the manager of the company, overseeing all business operations. The company's address was initially located on Rue du Consulat in the French Concession. Because it was a newly established business, its operations were initially quite prosperous. However, as the number of competitors increased and the price of radios gradually fell, the company began to lose money. By the end of last year, the results of two years of business showed that there was not only no profit, but also a loss of 8,000 gold. After discussions among the shareholders, it was decided to continue operations in the hope of recovering the losses. Unexpectedly, the business in the first quarter of this year was even worse, and the losses were even greater. However, those in charge were still unaware of the situation and instead tried to revitalize the company by claiming to increase capital and expand the scope of business. After spreading rumors that the original address was insufficient, they moved the company to the Xinxin Company on Nanjing Road, the commercial center of the city, on October 1st. Immediately, Chen Zizhen and Liu Hesheng went around purchasing large quantities of goods from Chinese and Western companies specializing in radios and electrical materials on credit. They gave post-dated checks drawn on the Shanghai Bank or Tonghe Bank to pay for the goods. Most of the goods owners were influenced by their earlier rumors and felt that they were extravagant, so they deeply believed in them. However, after the 15th of November, the person in charge of the company suddenly closed the company without waiting for the checks to mature and hired an accountant to announce the liquidation in the newspaper. The goods owners then realized that they had been deceived. As a result, the managers of Philips, Feige, etc., Van Os Wang Jue, Yao Yuyuan, Zhang Zhihua, Zheng Wenyi, Lu Yubin, Yang Xuegeng, Wang Zhentang, Cai Xiangyu, Li Peihang, Chen Shengda, Sun Guangjun, Li Wenxiang, Ge Tai, Xu Qixia, Lin Peiqing, Wang Meiqin, and 26 other households jointly hired lawyer Chen Tingrui to file a criminal self-accusation with the First Special District Court against the company's shareholders and directors Zhou Xiaoqing and others for fraudulently obtaining property. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Huang Risheng opened the trial. All the plaintiffs unanimously appeared in court and stated that they had been defrauded of goods with bad checks without sufficient funds. They also presented the checks they held as evidence. The amount was approximately 27,000 to 28,000 yuan. Of the ten defendants, only Zhou Xiaoqing, Chen Zizhen, Lu Mujun, Zhang Junliang, Zhu Zhenlu, and Liu Hesheng voted. The accountant hired by the company also appeared in court to report the liquidation process, stating that the company had a total loss of more than 32,000 yuan and that the goods in stock were still worth more than 17,000 gold. Judge Huang then ordered the accountant to investigate and report in detail on two points: how many goods the company had purchased since moving to Nanjing Road and before the liquidation, how much had been sold, and whether there were any funds in the Shanghai Bank for the checks issued to the creditors. The case was then adjourned for another hearing.

Bandit Suppression Army Battalion Commander Flees to Shanghai with Public Funds

Detained and Transferred to the Public Security Bureau

Xin Fu, also known as Dehuang, a native of Xinning County, Guangdong, 26 years old, served as the commander of the second transportation battalion in the transportation department of the East Route Headquarters of the Five-Province Bandit Suppression Army in Fujian, Jiangxi, Guangdong, Hunan, and Hubei. On October 14th of this year, he was assigned by the commander of the general team, Sun Zhaoren, to take official documents to the military supply department of the Jiangxi Fuzhou Camp to receive 6,900 yuan of public funds to purchase military supplies. After Xin was ordered to Jiangxi, he received the full amount on the 16th of the same month. He did not follow the order to purchase the items but instead secretly fled to Shanghai with the funds, spending the public funds at will. The Beijing Office of the East Route Headquarters of the Five-Province Bandit Suppression Army learned of this and immediately reported it to the Capital Garrison Command and the Police Department for investigation and arrest. It was not until recently that Xin Fu was found to be hiding at No. 44 Garden Lane, Rue Pères, in the French Concession of Shanghai. As a result, the Beijing Office sent adjutant Zhang Naixin and detective Dai Wenshu from the Capital Police Department to Shanghai to report to the Shanghai Public Security Bureau and request assistance in the arrest. Wu Tiecheng, who also served as the director of the bureau, ordered the captain of the detective team, Fu Ying, and detectives Wei Feng and Du Jinxiang to go to the French police station with the people who came to report the case on the morning of the previous day and request that police officer Wu Jiahui be dispatched to arrest Xin Fu at No. 44 Garden Lane. Xin happened to be out visiting friends at No. 48 in the same lane, so they immediately rushed over and arrested Xin Fu. They also searched his residence and seized a current account passbook with a balance of 2,000 yuan from the Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank's Eight Immortals Bridge branch and two seals, one Xin's personal seal and the other Su Changgan's seal, which is the Shanghai Bank deposit account name. The Su surname seal and clothing baggage check passbook had been withdrawn to five hundred and fifty yuan, and there was still one thousand four hundred and fifty yuan. They were immediately brought into the French police station. According to Xin's confession, after being ordered to Fuzhou, Jiangxi, to receive military funds, he put 4,300 yuan in a leather box and deposited it in his apartment room. He took 2,300 yuan with him to buy things outside. When he returned to his apartment, he found that the leather box containing the funds was missing, and the soldier Zhang Yushan, who was with him, was also missing. This prevented him from returning to cancel the difference. He temporarily stayed in Shanghai. The police chief ordered him to be detained pending referral to the court for review. Yesterday, the police station transferred Xin Fu to the Criminal Division I of the Special District Court, where Judge Cao Junsheng held two hearings. The leader of the detective team of the Public Security Bureau, Wei Feng, submitted an official document requesting the transfer of the lawyer Zhao Chen, who was defending the case, to the police station, stating that the case was based on the report of the Public Security Bureau requesting the Police Department to assist in the arrest of the defendant for embezzling public funds. The Police Department did not object to the Public Security Bureau's request for the transfer to the Police Department. The court was requested to indicate its opinion. Then, an official from the Shanghai Public Security Bureau stated the case, and the court inquired of the defendant Xin Fu, who gave the same confession as he had in the police station. Judge Cao then ruled that the defendant Xin Fu be allowed to be taken away by the official from the Shanghai Public Security Bureau to be interrogated.

Ill-Fated Lovers on a Journey

Man and Woman Attempt Suicide, Man Dead, Woman Critical

At the Xinmin Hotel in Yingchunfang, Taixin Street, Hubei Road, at about 1:00 AM yesterday morning, a young man in a Western suit and a woman arrived to check in. The man claimed to be Xue Xueliang, 29 years old, from Gansu, a rice merchant, and the woman was Xue Shen, 25 years old. The hotel clerk led them to Room 16 and allowed them to stay. Xue immediately paid the room fee of one yuan and eight cents and instructed the tea boy not to disturb them so that they could sleep peacefully. The tea boy and others did not suspect anything because it was late at night, so they closed the door and left. Unexpectedly, they had not gotten up by about 12:00 PM yesterday. They planned to knock on the door to inquire but suddenly heard a groan coming from the room. Knowing that something was wrong, they quickly tried to open the door and enter, and they saw the man and woman lying horizontally on the bed, both with pale faces. They quickly reported to the police station and had the man and woman taken to the hospital for treatment by car. After examination, it was found that they had both swallowed poison. Two suicide notes were found beside them and taken back to the police station for safekeeping. The man had been poisoned for a long time and could not be saved. He died soon after, and his body was transferred to the coroner's office for autopsy. The woman's life was also hanging by a thread. The reason for the poisoning is unknown.

Yongfeng Exchange Operates as Usual

Yongfeng Exchange, located in Fuchengli, Tianjin Road, was established in the 14th year of the Guangxu reign of the Qing Dynasty and has been in business for 47 years, making it the oldest exchange in Shanghai. The original shareholders were Wang Fengnian's ancestor, a Ningbo merchant, Chen Qiushan's successor ancestor, a Shaoxing merchant, and the _ family. Chen recommended his nephew Chen Yizhai as the manager and his fellow villager Tian Qiyuan as the assistant manager. After September 18th and January 28th, Chen wanted to close Yongfeng due to the economic downturn, but Wang did not agree. As a result, at the end of the lunar year, Chen formally withdrew his shares and Wang continued to operate the business solely. However, due to the heavy burden of settling the accounts for the withdrawal of shares, it was impossible to clear them up in a short time. Therefore, the original managers Tian Qiyuan and Li Jisheng stayed at the exchange to settle the accounts, which has been going on for ten months. Wang repeatedly urged Tian and Li, and then formally entrusted an accountant to handle the settlement of accounts. Tian, in his capacity as manager representing Yongfeng, used Wang's three outstanding debts as a way to resist. Wang then filed a lawsuit in court based on Chen's evidence of withdrawing his shares, requesting confirmation that Chen Qiushan had withdrawn his shares and confirmation that the two managers, Tian and Li, had lost their management positions due to Chen's withdrawal of shares. For the sake of protecting his rights, he applied to the court for a preliminary injunction. On the morning of the 3rd of this month, the First Special District Court ruled to grant the preliminary injunction, which stated that before the end of the lawsuit between the two parties confirming the withdrawal of shares and dismissing the managers, the opposing parties could not represent Yongfeng Exchange in any legal act without the consent of the applicant and could not change or move the exchange's property, equipment, documents, account books, inventory, etc. The reason was roughly that in order to maintain the status quo of Yongfeng Exchange and to ensure future compulsory enforcement, it was necessary to prohibit Chen Qiushan and others from engaging in legal acts that were detrimental to the applicant or from changing or moving the exchange's property, equipment, documents, account books, and inventory. After Wang received the ruling, he entrusted a lawyer to send a letter to the opposing lawyer to formulate five articles on the method of preliminary injunction, which were roughly as follows: (1) All records of account books, issuance of notes, receipt and payment of cash, preparation of letters, and stamping of receipts and receiving letters should still be handled by the original management personnel and must be approved by Fengnian, and Fengnian or an accountant or clerk entrusted by Fengnian should add a private seal on it for certification. (2) Major matters such as the recovery of loans, the signing of contracts, the increase in outstanding overdrafts, and the establishment of new pledges and new loans must be requested Fengnian's consent in advance, and Fengnian must affix his private seal to indicate approval. (3) Deeds, bonds, stocks, and all vouchers and documents should be stored in a library. The opposing party should list two copies of the list, which should be verified by Fengnian, and both parties should affix their seals. One copy should be stored in the library, and one copy should be handed over to Fengnian. The keys should be held by each party, and both parties should seal them to prevent changes or movements. (4) At the end of each day, the silver ocean should be checked against the inventory book, and the vault keys should be held by each party. The vault should be opened jointly the next day to prevent changes or movements. (5) All seals, account books, and all documents must be jointly kept by both parties to prevent changes or movements. The intention was to make all future actions of Yongfeng Exchange open to the public so that they could be supervised to avoid unexpected infringements. After the letter was sent, Chen and Tian did not reply and filed an appeal against the preliminary injunction. On the 6th of this month, the original court ruled to change the original ruling and rejected the application for a preliminary injunction. Wang obtained the ruling on the preliminary injunction for only three days before the original ruling was changed, so he was deeply shocked. He plans to file an appeal immediately to seek relief. At the same time, Yu Qiaqing and Qin Runqing believe that the situation is escalating, which is not a blessing for both parties, and plan to find a way to mediate.

The words "Beijing" are crossed out and the words "Shanghai" are printed

The printed notes have all been used up. The ordered notes have not yet arrived in Shanghai. In order to meet the urgent needs of society, we have changed the Beijing denomination one-yuan notes that our bank has printed and is awaiting release to Shanghai denomination, added the Shanghai note signature, and issued them immediately in order to speed up the process. The style is the same as the Shanghai one-yuan notes, but the color is slightly different. All Chinese and Western Beijing denominations on the front and back have been crossed out with several black lines and changed to print the words 'Shanghai'. They are used in the same way as the Shanghai denomination notes. We have sent a sample of the front and back on one piece of paper each. Please check and keep it. When the notes are on the counter, please use them in the same way as the original Shanghai one-yuan notes. We are very grateful for your public relations." The association has approved this and has pasted the sample in the market to facilitate the identification and use of members.

National Products Fair for Women Holds National Products Trademark Exhibition

Held at the Education Center starting on the 14th

The Shanghai Women's National Products Year Movement Committee has been holding national products mobile exhibitions in various schools since September 18th of this year, which have lasted for more than three months. Sixteen schools have been exhibited, and all have achieved excellent results. Recently, the association, in view of the approaching end of the year, in order to continue to work hard to arouse the public's use of national products, has specifically designated the Shanghai Public Education Center on Wenmiao Road in Nanshi to hold a national products trademark sample exhibition for three days starting on the 14th of this month. It is also scheduled to hold a national products circulation exhibition and a tea party for representatives of various factories at the association at 2:00 PM today to discuss the progress of the event. The exhibition methods are as follows: (1) All manufacturers participating in the national products trademark sample exhibition, regardless of whether their products are machine-made, handmade, or sold, must adhere to the principle of national products. (2) This exhibition is divided into two types: trademark exhibition and sample exhibition. The goods will be displayed in the same place at the same time to make it easier for visitors to identify and remember. (3) The aforementioned trademark exhibition will display objects divided into six types: patterns, sample photos, certificates, physical styles, and event life (each factory must have at least two types of patterns and physical styles when participating). All of these will be prepared by the manufacturers themselves. The sample exhibition must bring products with this trademark, regardless of quantity, and mark the product name, standard, brand, and raw material matching usage instructions, etc. The association will arrange the types of products according to the order of registration, designate the display location, and arrange them according to the address to show fairness. (4) The patterns and physical styles of the trademark exhibition display products must be of uniform size when drawn by each manufacturer. The association has specified the following: the pattern size is 2 feet long and 1.5 feet high, all mounted in black mirror cabinets; the physical style size is up to 2 feet in length, and the height and width are optional, but it must be convenient to carry and fold. (5) After the exhibition closes, the items on display, except for all samples, live animals, or other needed items, will be removed by the manufacturers. The remaining patterns, sample physical styles, and other trademarks will be collected by the association with the consent of the factory to be used for trademark exhibitions when the national products propaganda team departs to various places and villages, so that people in various places can recognize our national product trademarks. (6) Each manufacturer must send representatives to be responsible for the layout, display, transportation, and storage of the trademark samples at this exhibition. The association will not be responsible for any loss or damage. (7) The venue for this exhibition is the Dacheng Hall of the Public Education Center on Wenmiao Road in Nanshi, from December 14th to December 16th, 23rd year of the Republic of China, for three days. (8) The layout period for this exhibition is set for the day before the exhibition date. Each manufacturer must send the goods to the conference venue in advance and not be late. (9) All manufacturers who wish to participate in this exhibition should first fill out a registration form and register at the association, No. 80 Hualong Road, in order to arrange the location. (10) This method may be revised at any time if there are any shortcomings.

French Concession Board of Directors Increases Wine Tax

Increases from One Liang to Five Liang Per Month

Wine Stores Ask for Assistance from the Citizens' Association

Xin Xin She says, Wan Shun Xin Store, No. 475 Rue Albert, French Concession, has recently been subjected to a sudden increase in wine tax by the French Concession Board of Directors. Starting from November, the tax has increased from one liang to five liang per month. The store owner, Chen Yunzhang, believes that the increase in wine tax is unreasonable and cannot afford it. He took a letter to the Eighth District Branch of the Second Special District Citizens' Association to request assistance. The original letter is recorded as follows: "Dear committee members, please note that the wine tax on our small store has been increased out of the blue. The usual wine tax is one liang of silver per month, which is equivalent to 1.4 yuan in silver. Now, in November, it has suddenly increased by four liang of silver, making a total of five liang, which is equivalent to seven yuan in silver. However, our small store is very small, with only one shopfront, located at No. 475 Rue Albert in the French Concession. But this place is extremely deserted, and business is very small. Therefore, it is difficult to maintain even without an increase in wine tax, and it is even more difficult with an increase. The wine tax is suddenly increased, and the monthly earnings are not enough to pay the tax, which is less than seven yuan. In addition, we requested the members of the Eighth District Branch to go to the General Office of the Municipal Council the other day to request an exemption from the increase, but the General Office replied that they would send someone to investigate and then talk about it. Today, December 5th, the Municipal Council sent a letter stating that if the increased amount is not paid within five or six days, they will send someone to cut off the electricity wires at our small store. However, our small store has never owed any electricity fees to the electricity company. The Municipal Council is completely using coercive measures to deal with merchants. We are writing to request your association to uphold justice, negotiate on the basis of reason, and exempt us from the increased wine tax and unreasonable cutting off of electricity wires in order to maintain the difficult business."

Fire on Pushan Road, Zhabei

At 12:20 PM yesterday, a fire broke out at the home of Wang Shi, an elderly Shaoxing woman, at No. 1 Dehe Lane, Pushan Road, Zhabei, because she left the fire unattended outside the stove while cooking. In an instant, thick smoke billowed out, and flames soared, completely destroying the bungalow she lived in and spreading to the adjacent houses at No. 3 and No. 5. The fire brigade rushed to the scene and extinguished the fire at 1:30 PM.

Pharmacy Owner Acquitted in Lawsuit

Legally Responsible Person to Bear Criminal Responsibility

Shao Sunshi, wife of Shao Zhiying, a local resident of No. 283 Zhiren Lane, Kaizi'er Road, French Concession, suffered postpartum blood collapse in September of this year. Shao engaged traditional Chinese medicine doctor Zhou Weiqing for treatment. After examination, Dr. Zhou prescribed a blood-tonifying formula, instructing her to take one dose first and then return for a revised prescription. Shao took the prescription to Wang Tianfu Tang Chinese medicine store at the intersection of Xixinqiao Street, Fama Road, French Concession (the store had been open for decades and recently moved to Lucha Garden Road, Jiumu, after the lease expired; it had not been open for long). She bought two doses of medicine and took them home. After taking one dose, her condition not only did not improve but worsened. Shao urgently called Dr. Zhou again for examination and also examined the dregs. He discovered that the Puhuang carbon and Chen'ai carbon were not properly roasted or dried. Because raw ingredients cannot tonify blood but can stop blood, Shao immediately asked the doctor to prescribe another formula to remedy her condition. Meanwhile, she engaged lawyer Peng Qixiu to file a suit in the Special Court against Wang Futang, the owner of Wang Tianfu Tang pharmacy, for negligent business practices causing injury, based on Article 301 of the Criminal Law, requesting legal investigation and also filing a civil suit to recover losses. The court, after receiving the suit, ordered Judge Sun Peng to open a court session to summon and interrogate witnesses and verify the case. Yesterday morning, a continued trial was held, still presided over by Judge Sun in the criminal court. The defendant arrived with his defense lawyer, Zhu Taiqing. According to Wang's statement, "I do not manage the counter dispensing of medicine, and I was also unaware that the plaintiff came to collect the medicine. Therefore, I cannot be responsible for what the plaintiff accused." Then, witness Luo Jizhang, an apprentice, testified, "I do not manage the packaging of medicine; I only manage roasting the medicine." Witness Cao Yi also testified, "I work as a clerk at Wang Tianfu Tang. On September 19th, someone came to get two doses of medicine. I dispensed it, roasting both the Puhuang and Chen'ai thoroughly and putting them in. The boss does not manage packaging the medicine on the counter." The defendant, Wang Futang, also stated, "The plaintiff and I do not know each other, and the plaintiff is also from a pharmacy background and is now unemployed. Her purpose in suing me is to extort money." Upon hearing this, the plaintiff requested the court clerk to record Wang's statement clearly. The court then immediately began the debate and declared it closed, immediately acquitting the defendant and transferring the attached civil lawsuit to the civil court for trial. The judge also explained the meaning of the verdict to both parties, saying that the person packaging the medicine was not the defendant in this case and that the subject of the lawsuit was wrong. The legally responsible person must bear criminal responsibility. The plaintiff did not sue the defendant's employee before the debate concluded, so the defendant was acquitted.

Impersonating a Court Investigator to Extort Money

Huang Wanfang, who runs a clothing store on Daji Road outside the West Gate, has recently been involved in a lawsuit with others in the District Court that has not yet concluded. Yesterday afternoon, Lou Caihua, a Shaoxing native, suddenly arrived at the store, claiming to be an investigator from the District Court and demanding an investigation fee of several yuan. Huang Wanfang, knowing that the court does not charge such fees, clearly suspected impersonation and fraud. He pretended to comply and offered him cigarettes. Lou, seeing Huang's accommodating attitude, became complacent and began to brag. Unexpectedly, Huang ordered his apprentice to sound the alarm, and Lou was arrested and taken to the Ximen Branch Bureau. During interrogation, he confessed to selling old books. Today, he visited a friend in the area and used deceitful words to defend himself. Because the suspect dared to impersonate a public official and extort money, which is extremely illegal, it was immediately ordered that the suspect Lou Caihua be escorted to the District Court with documentation, requesting punishment according to the law to serve as a warning to others.

Famous Hong Lok Yuen Olives Arrive in Shanghai

Hong Lok Yuen, located in Tai Po, New Territories, Hong Kong, covers thousands of acres and is the largest fruit orchard in our country. It is carefully cultivated by experienced fruit tree experts using scientific methods. The famous fruits produced number in the hundreds, with olives being the best. Olives with small spots on the skin are especially good. They are sweet and fragrant, without any impurities. Eating them daily is beneficial to health. Tang Hanwen Declared Not Guilty Yesterday

Lawyer Yu Xiangqin Vigorously Defends

Xinmin News reports that Tang Hanwen and Shen Shizhong, who were wrongly convicted and sentenced to one year and nine months in prison in the Clark Road Jingxin Printing Press robbery case in May of this year, were defended by their lawyer Yu Xiangqin, who presented the points of false accusation in detail and appealed to the Second Branch of the High Court. After three investigation court sessions, the truth of the case was revealed. November 30th was the date of the appeal court hearing. Presiding Judge Guo Dezhang presided over the court and inquired in detail. The lawyer Yu presented the reasons for the appeal and the points of false accusation in detail, stating roughly that the appellant makes a living as a butcher, with monthly income ranging from one hundred and several tens of yuan to seven hundred yuan. Therefore, it is difficult to believe that he would give up his good business and covet a mere five yuan to commit robbery. If it is said to be the money from sharing the spoils, then why did Wang Meisheng and Chen Zhikang each get sixteen yuan, while the appellant only got five yuan? It can be seen that although the patrol room used torture to extract a confession and fabricate a crime, there were still loopholes to be found. Upon inspecting the Jingxin Printing Press, no one was seen holding a handgun at the time of the incident. The patrol room did not find a handgun at the appellant's place or at the Lu's place. Both parties in the confession also said that they did not carry a handgun. Therefore, there was no murder weapon in this case, and the so-called aiding and abetting robbery with a weapon is completely unfounded. Upon inspecting the defendants related to this case, they all stated that they had "never seen each other and did not know each other," which further proves that the appellant was not involved in this case, etc. At this point, the debate concluded. Yesterday was the date of the sentencing. Presiding Judge Guo Dezhang still presided over the court, inquired briefly, and then acquitted Tang Hanwen and Shen Shizhong in court. After the verdict was announced, the court adjourned.

The Crisis of China and the World (4)

Lecture by Dr. Eddy, recorded by Bingxun Quick Recording Society, Shen Wan Quick Recording

In Beiping, I met Dr. Hu Shi, who said that China needs social reform. He also said, "Some places in China still have the bad habits of foot-binding." The way they walk is awkward and delicate. This bad habit not only restricts their bodies but also their minds. Japanese women walk freely, and women all over the world walk freely. Why are Chinese women so restricted in their walking? From a political, intellectual, moral, economic, and social point of view, China urgently needs new people and new methods to lead the people. Now, I have a question to ask: are we new leaders? Are we sound? Can we save China? If not, what is the reason? Let me give you a few examples. When I arrived in Tianjin, I saw that the shops in the Japanese concessions were selling heroin, morphine, and other drugs to numb the people of North China. And when I went to ____, I saw that people were addicted to opium. The smoky, hazy scene blurred the entire North China. Here is a photo of an eleven-year-old, who also died from taking Japanese drugs. Here is also a photo of five hundred opium addicts, also poisoned by the Japanese. But even more terrible than this poison is that the Chinese themselves grow opium. In Sichuan, I could buy opium anytime, anywhere, like buying bread, selling it package by package. Anyone could buy it, even children. How can we save China like this? There is also something ten times more detestable than the Japanese poisoning North China, and that is corruption. Corruption can destroy the army, corrupt the government, and lead to the failure of businesses. I once saw in Henan a coal-producing area with very rich annual output. Initially, the mine was run by foreigners, with only a few dozen people in charge, and they made a lot of money. Later, the Chinese took it back and operated it, employing six hundred people to manage it. These six hundred people were all their relatives and friends, all embracing the principle of corruption. Originally, they could earn 130,000 yuan each year, but at the end of the year, the accounts showed a loss of 2 million yuan. Soon, it was about to go bankrupt. Later, when Chairman Chiang Kai-shek found out, he sent people to reorganize it and dismissed the six hundred administrative personnel, reorganizing it. By the end of the second year, they had earned back 1.3 million yuan. China has always had silk, tea, and ____ as major export items. Where are China's exported silk and tea now? China has always exported tea, but now its markets have been seized by India, Japan, and Ceylon. There was a province where the government allocated 200,000 to 250,000 yuan to help the rural areas. This amount was spent in five parts, but four-fifths of the money was used for the people, and the remaining one-fifth went into their own pockets. The agricultural tools purchased were not good, and the farmers did not get any benefit. Is this still considered helping the rural areas? This kind of corrupt behavior is plundering the lifeblood of the country. There was a ____ in Rehe, governed by a very fat general. He had many motorcades and many concubines, but one hundred and forty-eight Japanese soldiers drove him away. If this corrupt system is not changed, China will never have hope. Thirty years ago, when I lectured in the north, many students listened to my lectures. When they heard about the revolution, everyone applauded greatly. However, because they were dishonest, they became officials themselves and were even more corrupt than the officials of the Qing Dynasty. Now, I ask you, are you honest? Are you clean? I will give two examples, one of honesty and one of dishonesty. The honest person is George Washington, who did many great things in American history. And a dishonest person is ____. Previously, there was a very smart student in Peiping who thought he could save China. He could give speeches and often used the Three Principles of the People as his slogan. Later, he became an official and earned 500 yuan a month. After that, the government sent him abroad. He stayed in very aristocratic hotels and told many lies. Later, the government found out and dismissed him from his post. As a result, he became unemployed and ended up in Shanghai as a ____ bandit. This is the result of dishonesty. Ladies and gentlemen, the Chinese are a pile of loose sand, only knowing selfishness and self-interest, only knowing corruption. Can this kind of dishonesty save China? Can the country be saved if they are always drunk and dreaming? Are you honest? Is your mind pure? Can you save the country? We all know that loose sand cannot be combined. We need to use cement to solidify it. Can it be that we rational human beings cannot unite? We must be as hard as stone, using inner and outer efforts to save China, to cope with the major crisis facing China and the world today. (The End)

Education News

National Vocational Education Conference Opened Yesterday

Minister of Education Wang Gave a Speech, Director Gu Reported

Nine Proposals from the Ministry of Education and More Than Twenty Other Proposals

-Resolved: Each Department and Bureau Should Establish a Specialist to Handle Vocational Education-

-Ministry of Education's Vocational Education Laws and Regulations Urging Implementation Methods-

(Nanjing, 7th Dispatch) The National Vocational Education Discussion Conference opened at 9:00 AM on the 7th at the Ministry of Education. Representatives from education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities, and experts such as Jiang Hengyuan, etc., totaling fifty-seven people, attended.

Minister of Education Wang Gave a Speech

Minister of Education Wang presided over and gave a speech, saying, "In the past two or three years, the Ministry has felt various difficulties in the promotion and experimental experience of vocational education. The biggest ones are: 1. Funding, 2. Teachers, 3. Students' employment prospects, 4. Reasonable social transformation, etc. The Ministry has slightly organized plans for the above issues, urging various provinces and cities to earnestly implement the plans. However, whether these plans are feasible still requires further research. Therefore, we have specially invited experts and representatives from various provinces and cities to hold a vocational education discussion conference. We ask ____ to discuss the various plans of the Ministry, establish concrete plans, and the colleagues of the Ministry will certainly try our best to improve and promote vocational education, reaching a broad road. I wish everyone success in their careers."

Director Gu's Report

After Wang finished his speech, he left the meeting and Gu Shusen took over as chairman, reporting on the nine proposals submitted by the Ministry of Education, divided into two groups, and explaining the content of the proposals. The more than twenty proposals from various provinces and cities were listed in a separate agenda. Additional proposals from various provinces and cities are being submitted today and are currently being printed. A total of more than fifty proposals, please discuss what kind of solution should be adopted.

Minister of Education Wang giving the opening speech at the National Vocational Education Conference (Photo taken in Nanjing Guanghua)

Discussion of Five Proposals

1. Resolved that all proposals should be submitted to the General Assembly for discussion. The nine proposals submitted by the Ministry of Education should be the basis and discussed in order. Other proposals related to the Ministry of Education's proposals may be added to the discussion ad hoc. If the General Assembly encounters difficulties that must be submitted for review, a review committee will be organized to resolve them.

2. Proposal that each provincial and municipal education department and bureau should establish full-time personnel to handle and inspect vocational education.

Resolved A: At least one full-time person should be established in the department in charge of school education to handle vocational education and vocational guidance. B: One to two supervisors or instructors should be designated, and specialized talent should be hired temporarily to inspect vocational schools at all levels. C: Please instruct the Ministry of Education to order various provinces and cities to realize this method as soon as possible.

3. How should each province and city implement the standards for the establishment and funding allocation of secondary schools set by the Ministry?

Resolved A: The Jiangsu Province proposal to promote vocational education, with the standard for funding allocation accounting for at least 35% of secondary education funding, and whether it can reach the standard as scheduled, it is proposed to consider the reality and allow for flexibility, which should be incorporated into this discussion and a review committee should be organized. Members of the review committee are tentatively appointed: Lai Zhizhong, Li Fangyu, Yang Nai____, He Qingming, Zheng Tanchi, Gong Duzhan, Shi'an Lu Dianyuan, Cai Shufang, Zheng Tonghe, Zhang Shenyun, Huang Shuxuan, Yang Kejing, Ren ____, Bei Miaoyingtu ____, Ru Zhou Zhiguan, Zhang Chuanqi, Xu Zhi, Chen Bai, Xiao Shujiong, Yi Junreng, Jiang Hengyuan, Chen Shizhen, Dai ____ Guan ____ Daozan, to be convened by Zhong, and a meeting will be held at 9:00 AM on the 8th.

4. Regarding the laws and regulations on vocational education, how should their implementation be urged and what suggestions are there?

Resolved to pass the four measures after making revisions.

5. Regarding the types of departments to be established in existing vocational schools based on the industry status and the types of vocational talents needed in each province and city, the decision is to incorporate it into the funding allocation review committee for discussion.

6. The chairman proposed ad hoc to form another review committee on the issue of department establishment and curriculum in vocational schools and employment prospects for graduates. Meng ____ Zhou Shengtang, Chen Dejiong, Huang Zudu, Song Yuming, Chen Zhongrong, Luo Jingyuan, Fu Xueshi, Li Tanfu, He Tang, Wei Yuanguang, Zhang Bingwen, Zou Shuwen, Pi Zuoqiong, Fu Enxu, Yu Tongkui, He Qingru, Tang Yingzhang, Ji Nan Zhou Qinshu, Deng Bangdi, Tang Zhicai, Zheng Bijang, and Gu Ji were tentatively appointed as members, to be convened by Gu, and a meeting will be held at 9:00 AM on the 8th.

Entitled The Meaning and Function of Vocational Designation

Zhou Bohai, Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education, submitted the following four proposals to the General Assembly: (1) Request that the central government consider providing funding to reward outstanding vocational schools in various provinces and cities; (2) ____ List the practical training time of various vocational schools, please discuss and earnestly participate in the opinions and send them for reference and adoption; (3) Promote vocational education, with the standard for funding allocation accounting for at least 35% of secondary education funding, and whether it can reach the standard as scheduled, it is proposed to consider the facts and allow for flexibility; (4) ____ On the issue of Jiangsu Province's raw material production, please ask the central government to plan ____ factories to specially promote ____.

Jiangsu Province Vocational Education Report

The general situation report on vocational education of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education is as follows:

Jiangsu's handling of vocational education did not start today, roughly speaking, it has a history of twenty years. At its peak, there were more than two hundred and seventy A and B types of industrial schools in the province, and the vocational education attached to them is not included. As for the promotion and research of vocational education, considerable efforts have also been made, such as setting up vocational education instructors, holding meetings of principals of B-type industrial schools, and organizing the Provincial Vocational School Federation, all of which are manifestations of their efforts. Weighing the situation and measuring the reasons, the future of vocational education in Jiangsu should be very optimistic. However, until the reorganization of schools in 1927, elementary schools were uniformly changed to ordinary elementary schools, and B-type industrial schools ceased to exist due to this. The merger of secondary schools and normal schools affected A-type industrial schools. Only the four schools of Su Nong, Huai Nong, ____ Can, and Aquatic Products, as well as the two vocational departments of secondary schools, can survive independently. Considering the results, the reason why this happened is that the poor management of vocational education in the past really led to it. Analytically speaking, there are four points: (1) Due to the courses being too generalized, the courses of past vocational schools often leaned towards general subjects, and did not focus on skills training, resulting in their graduates not being as good as ordinary secondary school students in terms of scientific theory, and not as practical as farmers and workers in terms of vocational skills. They were often famous but not real; (2) Due to the lack of appropriate factory and farm equipment, past agricultural and industrial vocational schools also had attached farms and factories, but either the sites were too small or the equipment was incomplete, and they were only used for students' experiments. In fact, the results of the experimental work, even the best ones, were only like the science experiment rooms of ordinary secondary schools, which could be used for teachers' explanations; (3) Due to the lack of importance attached to the operation of agricultural and industrial farms, the lack of equipment in agricultural and industrial farms was as described above, and vocational school teachers were also mostly confined to old habits, able to speak but unable to do, and the basic practical work of agricultural and industrial farms was mostly done by agricultural workers hired by the school. Students only learned from the examples of farmers and workers in agricultural and industrial farms, and teachers mostly stood by and supervised. Teachers and students lacked basic production skill training in agricultural and industrial farms; (4) Due to the lack of close contact between schools and the vocational industry, past vocational schools specialized in teaching and rarely had close contact with enterprises of the same nature, so the skills trained by schools were not linked to the actual needs of the vocational industry, resulting in extreme difficulties in the employment prospects of graduates. For these reasons, although vocational education in Jiangsu once started for a while, it ultimately failed to achieve significant results, and the credibility of the society was not established. ____ As the days went by, it became even more alienated, and it fell to an all-time low, which is also a matter of course.

In the spring of 1931, the Ministry of Education, in view of the abnormal expansion of ordinary secondary schools in recent years, the number of secondary school graduates has increased sharply, but only a few of them can go on to higher education. Those who cannot go on to higher education also lack the training in appropriate production skills and cannot engage in appropriate occupations to earn an independent living. If we do not seek relief urgently, it will be a hidden danger for the society and the country. Therefore, the Ministry issued Instruction No. 536, restricting the establishment of ordinary secondary schools, increasing vocational schools, adding vocational departments or vocational subjects in ordinary secondary schools, and county-run ____ secondary schools should be attached to or converted into rural normal schools and vocational departments, and Instruction No. 1436, issuing the implementation plan for the establishment of secondary agricultural and industrial schools in various provinces and cities. After receiving the order, the Department of Education immediately examined the actual situation of secondary education in Jiangsu Province and actively followed the instructions. Later, in September 1931, Instruction No. 19736 was received, issuing the standards and methods for the establishment and funding allocation of secondary schools in various provinces and cities. It was found that the number of vocational schools in Jiangsu Province had sharply decreased since the reorganization of schools in 1927, and has gradually increased again in recent years, aiming to reach the standards stipulated by the Ministry by 1937. However, it is still uncertain whether it can be fully realized according to the planned plan. The progress of provincial vocational schools in recent years is reported in numbers as follows: In 1930, there were four vocational schools and two vocational departments in secondary schools, which was the same as in 1927, with a total of nine departments and thirty-seven classes, and a recurrent expenditure of 238,802 yuan, accounting for 13.61% of the total recurrent expenditure of secondary education. By 1931, there were five vocational schools and four vocational departments in secondary schools, with a total of eleven departments and forty-two classes, and a recurrent expenditure of 19.79 yuan, accounting for 15.65% of the total, an increase of 2.05% compared to 1930, totaling 51,990 yuan. By 1932, there were six vocational schools and four vocational departments in secondary schools, with a total of three departments and forty classes, and a recurrent expenditure of 332,435 yuan, accounting for 17.21% of the total, an increase of 1.56% compared to five years, totaling 41,643 yuan. By 1933, there were six vocational schools, plus one public school, and four vocational departments in secondary schools, with a total of fourteen departments and fifty-one schools, and a recurrent expenditure of 411,841 yuan, accounting for 19.23% of the total, an increase of 1.01% compared to 1932, totaling 75,406 yuan. By 1934, there were nine vocational schools and three vocational departments in secondary schools, with a total of seventeen departments and fifty-four classes, and a recurrent expenditure of 551,624 yuan, accounting for 25.31% of the total, an increase of 6.08% compared to 1933, totaling 139,783 yuan. The number of temporary expenses allocated over the years is not included. This is only for the progress of provincial vocational schools in recent years. Furthermore, in terms of the situation of county and private vocational schools, the financial situation of county secondary schools in Jiangsu Province is more complicated, and each county has more ____ special histories. If it must be handled in accordance with the financial distribution standards for secondary schools promulgated by the Ministry, there will inevitably be many difficulties. Because the education budget of each county in Jiangsu Province has always been divided into administrative expenses, general education expenses, compulsory education expenses, and social education expenses, the expenses of senior elementary schools, ordinary secondary schools, and vocational schools belong to general education expenses, and the expenses of primary elementary schools and normal education belong to compulsory education expenses. In order to prevent encroachment, the funds of each item must not be misappropriated arbitrarily. If we want to overturn the established practice and redistribute it, difficulties will inevitably arise. In addition, the secondary education funds of each county are limited. Within a county, it is rare to run secondary schools, normal schools, and vocational schools at the same time. Therefore, in terms of funding allocation, it is difficult to meet the standards promulgated by the Ministry anyway. Due to the lack of ____ methods, we came up with a remedy, which is to restrict the expansion of county and private secondary schools arbitrarily, promote vocational schools at all levels, and actively promote them. We have formulated specific measures and notified various counties: (1) County-run secondary schools that originally ran on a single-track system must not expand classes under the pretext of a large number of students going on to higher education. Those that originally ran on a single-track system will gradually reduce enrollment from 1934 and be converted into a single-track system by 1937; (2) Counties that already run vocational schools should find ways to expand them, and those that have not yet run them should prepare to establish them immediately. The funds should be offset by the reduced secondary schools or newly added funds. In case the funds are limited, vocational supplementary schools should also be set up to train production skills for students who cannot go on to higher education; (3) Private secondary schools that have been established and are located in areas with a large number of ordinary secondary schools should be urged and persuaded to reduce ordinary classes and gradually convert to vocational schools or vocational supplementary schools; (4) Since ____, individuals who are preparing to establish secondary schools should be urged and persuaded to convert to vocational schools or vocational supplementary schools. If the funds are not very abundant, they should be directly persuaded to convert to elementary schools to show restrictions. Since the order was issued, it has been quite effective. It is estimated that in 1930, there were only three county-run vocational schools and four private vocational schools. By 1934, the number of county-run vocational schools had increased to eleven and the number of private vocational schools had increased to fourteen. This is the general situation of the promotion of vocational education in various counties by the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education in recent years in accordance with the Ministry's instructions.

The above is in terms of the increase in the number of vocational schools. In terms of the qualitative improvement, we have already seen the reasons for the failure of vocational education in the past. This time, we are not ____ a second experiment. From a negative point of view, how should we try to avoid all the past misfortunes so that they do not reappear? From a positive point of view, how should we plan to be perfect and open up new paths to obtain better results? Our responsibilities lie in this, and we must always keep this in mind. The main points of the improvement plan implemented in the past three years are described below to see the general class of attention to improvement at ordinary times. According to this plan, there are still those who continue to promote it.

A. Regarding agricultural schools: (1) Pay attention to vocational goals, revise curriculum standards, so that the focus of the curriculum is on vocational training, not on cultivating higher education. In order to achieve this goal, take centralized basic training, add knowledge of specialized studies as needed, and increase the amount of practical skill training to arouse students' interest in farming; (2) Focus on agricultural product manufacturing and gradually enrich agricultural product processing equipment; (3) Pay attention to promoting cooperative business, in order to ____ make schools and rural life a whole.

B. Regarding sericulture schools: (1) Improve seed production and silk reeling, proceed simultaneously, and at the same time promote the results obtained in their ____ experimental institute in the sericulture industry, so that schools and the sericulture industry become a whole; (2) Pay off all the old loans of the old factory owners of the school in one lump sum, in order to increase the credibility of the school and the factory owners.

C. Regarding agricultural and sericultural research and experimental institutions, it is planned to unite the agricultural colleges of various famous universities in the capital and this province, guiding institutes, experimental farms, and ____ affiliated agricultural and sericultural schools to organize agricultural and sericultural research institutions, classify them by category, and engage in research, experiments, and guidance on various improvement matters in agricultural farms.

D. Regarding aquatic product schools: (1) Add all application instruments to enhance the effectiveness of education; (2) Set up ways to ____ set up trawls within possible scope, so that students can get full benefits from fishery practice; (3) ____ Order the school to make full use of the school's canning and ____ factory equipment, and strive to increase the efficiency and income of the internship every day; (4) Encourage the school to continue to work hard and maintain close contact with the fishing industry.

E. Regarding industrial schools (1) Continue to complete the equipment of the workshops of various industrial schools to increase the teaching and internship efficiency of each school, and actively find ways to focus on the production of school workshops, so that the manufacturing cost is reduced and the shipping standards are increased. ____ The workshop's own business has therefore developed day by day. In terms of employees, there are also profit-sharing incentive methods to meet the principles of business economics; (3) Students in the factory practice are completely the same as ordinary workers. Unless they absolutely obey the orders of the technicians, they are not allowed to enter the factory to work.

F. Regarding commercial schools, we adopt a centralized enrichment method. The provincial school's senior high school commercial department is responsible for the provincial Shanghai High School to handle, and actively enrich the equipment, such as the storage of internship bank funds, the actual operation of small-scale asset consumption cooperation, and the equipment of the commodity display room are all organized according to actual needs, distinguishing between urgency and priority.

Most recently, in November, a conference of principals of provincial vocational schools in the province was convened. Issues such as the employment prospects of graduates, subject teaching materials, the amount of internship, and the contact between the ____ department and enterprises of the same department were all discussed in detail and plans were formulated for adoption. These are all related to the qualitative improvement of vocational education.

Education is the whole problem of the country, and vocational education is no exception. Moreover, in terms of the essence of vocational education, the development of agriculture, industry, and commerce is the foundation. In terms of a province, it is not possible to achieve perfection unless the four industries of ____ people, finance, education, and construction are truly integrated and jointly planned. At present, although Jiangsu Province has not yet promulgated regulations on the joint handling of vocational education by other departments and the Department of Education, in fact, it already has the trend of an invisible alliance between the four industries of people, finance, education, and construction. There are many examples, such as the former Industry Department allocating textile finishing machinery to the dyeing and weaving factory of Suzhou Industrial School. Some of the Construction Department has also designated several farms, and the Department of Education has ordered the county education bureaus where they are located to formulate a reorganization plan to be responsible for the handling. The Land Bureau is carrying out the land survey and measurement business, and Suzhou Industrial School is training talents for it and borrowing instruments. The relationship between each other is getting deeper and deeper. The Finance and Construction Departments recently consulted with the Department of Education on the establishment of a training farm for agricultural cooperation talents. ____ Suzhou and Huaiyin schools were ordered to select ____ agricultural students. These are all obvious ____ in people's ears and days. This spirit of union is progressing day by day, and it is the dawn of the future of vocational education in Jiangsu. What we can be gratified about is that ____ those who run vocational education in Jiangsu Province are unusually cautious in the past, and all promotion plans in recent years, or because of following the previous orders, or due to the special situation of the local area, may still be ____ compliant with the recent ministerial order urging various provinces and cities to promote vocational education methods, and we still ask ____ to give a preliminary review and remove ____ opinions. In addition to submitting another proposal, we will also report the facts truthfully. ____ Is there any need for review? The person in charge of vocational education at the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education, Xiang Shaoxuan.

National Labor Exhibition, Day 7

Sixty-Three Groups Visited Yesterday

The Number of People Reached More Than Three Thousand One Hundred

(Nanjing, 7th Dispatch) A total of sixty-three schools and groups, with three thousand one hundred and seventy-eight people, visited the National Vocational Education and Labor Exhibition on the 7th.

Labor Exhibition Investigation Record

The National Vocational School and Primary and Secondary School Labor Course Achievement Exhibition, organized by the Ministry of Education in its 23rd year, opened on the 1st of this month. The preparations and the visits from various sectors in recent days have been reported in various newspapers. This reporter has conducted a detailed investigation and contacted the relevant staff, obtaining materials that can be used as a systematic record. Therefore, I am writing this report to share with fellow journalists, hoping to be the first to present it.

(1) Preparation Situation

The exhibition was originally scheduled to be held on October 10th. In mid-July, five preparatory committee members, Tang Xifen, Gu Zhaolin, Zhou Bangdao, Dai Yingqin, and Zhong Daozan, were appointed to take charge. However, borrowing venues such as the Lishi Society, YMCA, Zhongren Sports Field, and Overseas Chinese Reception Center was unsuccessful, and the Chaoda Palace was in a dilapidated state, impossible to repair. It was difficult to find a suitable venue, and the preparations almost came to a halt. Finally, it was discovered that the Examination Yuan examination hall would be available in mid-November, and the new building of the Ministry of Transportation was completed and could be used as the exhibition venue. The preparatory committee members then negotiated separately. Eventually, with the special approval of President Dai Jitao, it was decided to use the Examination Yuan examination hall. The examination hall was magnificent and meticulously built, and measures had to be taken to protect the windows and floors from damage. At this time, the number of preparatory committee members had been increased to sixteen, and five standing committee members were appointed to oversee the overall situation. After multiple discussions, it was generally agreed that carpets had to be laid and displays arranged along the interior and exterior edges to prevent damage to the floors, doors, and windows. Otherwise, with tens of thousands of visitors walking and crowding inside every day, it would be difficult to guarantee that there would be no damage. The standing committee members of the association put a lot of effort into protecting the examination hall. As a result, the expenditure on protecting the building reached as much as two thousand yuan, showing the importance attached to public property.

The most difficult problem for the association, besides the venue address, was the display cabinets for the exhibits. Custom-made cabinets would not only have uncertain costs but also be limited by time. Simple cabinets would not be aesthetically pleasing, while elaborate ones would be too expensive. Therefore, the eighty-three newly manufactured steel cabinets from the Vocational Education Exhibition were borrowed in their entirety. The Railway Department provided free transportation from Tianjin to Beijing, and the association only paid for the ferry fee of 156 yuan. The installation was also undertaken by workers dispatched by the Railway Department, which was very convenient. In addition, the association custom-made 180 trapezoidal stands, 80 picture stands, 300 wooden stands, and some wooden boards, spending a total of 1,300 to 1,400 yuan. After the closing of the exhibition, the trapezoidal stands could be used by small merchants to display goods and by households to display potted flowers, and the hanging stands could be converted into bookshelves, so that they would not be completely useless. The design was carefully considered. The association first installed all kinds of display cabinets, and then invited representatives from various provinces and the exhibition committee members to jointly display the exhibits. At the same time, many temporary workers were needed, and the venue was bustling. The exhibits were arranged according to the regulations of the Ministry of Education, first vocational, then secondary, and then primary. Because the styles and structures of the exhibits were very complex, classification was quite difficult. The display started on November 13th and lasted until the 18th, a total of five days, during which all the pavilions completed their arrangements. The representatives from various provinces and the exhibition committee members worked hard, and their insights were extremely rich. They even added night shifts twice to rush the work to completion, which shows how intense the work was. Finally, on the 29th and 30th, the entire preparatory committee, together with the representatives from various provinces, jointly inspected and reorganized the order. The display work was then completed. The Vice Minister and Chief Secretary of the Ministry even personally inspected the venue for a week, which shows that the Ministry attached great importance to this exhibition.

(2) Financial Situation

The association's budget, before the venue was determined, was estimated at over 11,000 yuan, all of which was saved from expenses in order to make ends meet. After the venue was determined, one was the cost of protecting the examination hall building, which was about two thousand yuan, and the other was the cost of careful arrangement and striving for order, which was about four or five hundred yuan more. The third was that, because the examination hall was borrowed, at least half of the water and electricity fees had to be paid, which was about three or four hundred yuan. These two items were about three thousand yuan. In addition, there were slight increases in items such as the installation of a wireless radio receiver and the custom-made badges. The wooden frames made by the various pavilions for special exhibits also accounted for a portion of the expenses, thus consuming several hundred yuan. The exhibition period was originally scheduled for ten days, but it has now been extended by two days, plus two days for judging, for a total of fourteen days, which will also require increased expenditures. All of these were not included in the original budget, and the committee members are trying to tighten their belts in order to avoid exceeding the budget too much. The venue layout has already been completed. The major expenses after this will be the aftercare, salaries, printing, and organization, which are relatively large. The reporter has seen the standing committee members of the association walking back and forth from the Ministry of Education to the Examination Yuan in recent days, which shows the extent of their frugality.

(3) Organizational Situation

The organization of the association is a preparatory committee, with five standing committee members appointed by the Minister. Underneath it are two committees, the Exhibition and Arrangement Committee and the Judging Committee, and two groups, the General Affairs Group and the Editorial Group, each with a director. The director of the Exhibition and Arrangement Committee is Inspector Tang Xifen, the director of the Judging Committee is Si Gu Shusen, the director of the General Affairs Group is Inspector Gu Zhaolin, and the director of the Editorial Group is Inspector Zhou Bangdao. Under the groups are sections, with section chiefs and staff members, mostly concurrently held by members of the Ministry, with only a few outsiders. The exhibition committee members are concurrently held by the preparatory committee members, and representatives and other members of the Ministry also serve as staff members. The members of the Judging Committee are experts from the education and business sectors who have been invited to serve, and more than ten people have been internally appointed and are currently seeking their consent. The General Affairs Group has a general secretary and a general affairs, accounting, and reception section. During the exhibition period, the representatives from various provinces serve as reception staff, and the rest are staffed by members of the Ministry on a rotational basis, with two people in each pavilion. During the opening period, there are two general commanders in the venue, Hao Gengsheng, who is responsible for leading the venue staff and the Boy Scouts to maintain order throughout the venue. Since the opening, the situation has been different. In addition to the full attendance of all standing committee members every day, all preparatory committee members and staff members take turns to go to take care of things, so that when special circumstances arise, they can find ways to help at any time. According to Gu Zhaolin, the director of general affairs of the association, the order outside the door on the mornings of the 1st and 2nd was not good, and the staff issuing tickets did not handle the situation properly. Additional staff have now been assigned to correct the situation. However, many of the staff members in the association are concurrently employed and not enough to allocate, and limited by funding, they cannot increase the number of staff. We hope that all sectors will forgive any shortcomings that arise." His words expressed a sense of sadness, which shows that the handling of affairs is not without difficulties.

(4) Venue Situation

The layout of the venue is generally tidy, but the turns in the second and fourth pavilions are too narrow, and the audience is prone to crowding. Many people from all walks of life have also mentioned this point in their criticisms in recent days. The person in charge of the association said that the aisles in the venue were originally designed to be four feet wide, enough for three people to pass through, but because the venue was small and the exhibits sent by the provinces were too many, it was not convenient to reduce the size of the exhibits. Therefore, the number of wooden frames was repeatedly increased, resulting in slightly narrower aisles, which was a last resort. However, even with this arrangement, only three-quarters of the original exhibits could be displayed, and one-quarter could not be accommodated. "If the aisles are widened for the convenience of pedestrians, what will be the basis for judging?"

Although the audience has been very crowded in recent days, the order in the venue can still be maintained with effort. However, on the morning of the 2nd, a woman fainted in the first pavilion and was rescued out of the venue by the Boy Scouts. Also, a child fell under a wooden frame on the podium of the fourth pavilion and was helped up by a representative from Hubei. Also, a staff member lost a pen, which was picked up and returned by a worker. Also, the Qingdao City lost a pair of gloves, and Jiangsu Province lost a clock. At that time, there were still no major losses. In addition, there is too much dust in the venue, which is indeed a shortcoming. According to the management staff of the association, "The venue is swept once every day after closing the door, and sometimes a night shift is added. The cleaning is completed at four o'clock in the morning every night, which cannot be said to be insufficient. But after ten o'clock in the morning, the dust rises again. The reason is that the floating dust under the shoes of the audience flies up, which is difficult to prevent. Now the windows and doors cannot be closed, so the electric fans on the walls can only be turned on and off at any time to adjust the situation. We are currently thinking of various ways to facilitate the audience."

Chairman Chiang Kai-shek Subsidizes the Promotion of Vocational Education in Chahar Province

Allocates 100,000 Yuan to be Used for the Livestock Department and Afforestation of Vocational Schools

Wang Jiruo, Section Chief of the Chahar Provincial Department of Education, attended the National Vocational Education Discussion Meeting convened by the Ministry of Education. In a recent interview, he said that after Chairman Chiang Kai-shek inspected the province, he generously allocated 100,000 yuan annually from the Nanchang Headquarters (50,000 yuan has already been allocated), with 30,000 yuan for afforestation expenses, 20,000 yuan for running the livestock department of vocational schools, 10,000 yuan for subsidizing school military training, and 40,000 yuan for promoting mass education outside the pass. Currently, the Provincial Department of Education has opened a livestock department in vocational schools, and next year will continue to promote the school system for compulsory education, first running joint rural normal schools to train teachers and provide Mongolian language instruction to facilitate the promotion of primary schools outside the pass for the League Flag children. To promote mass education, it is planned to organize a mobile lecture tour group with several cars, divided into four departments: lecture, health, art, education, and film. They will set off for a 20-day mobile lecture tour in various places outside the pass every month. Such a method of promoting mass education is also a novel approach. It is also heard that representatives of the Provincial Department of Education have consulted with the Ministry of Education to introduce provinces and cities that have self-made educational films (such as Jiangsu) to rent more educational films and prepare to bring them to Chahar Province for application after the vocational education discussion meeting.

Second Preparatory Meeting of the London Chinese Art Exhibition Held Yesterday

A Preview Exhibition Will Be Held in Shanghai in March Next Year

(Nanjing, 7th) The London International Exhibition of Chinese Art held its second meeting on the 6th and resolved the following: (1) It was decided that a preview exhibition of the exhibits will be held in Shanghai in March next year; (2) The selection of exhibits will be the responsibility of a specialized committee; (3) The most important exhibits will be bronzes, porcelains, and paintings; (4) The exhibition will be limited to items from the Kangxi and Qianlong periods and earlier.

Fundraising for Disaster Relief Begins Today in the City's Education Sector

Principals, Teachers, and Students of All Large, Medium, and Small Schools in the City Will Begin a Campaign to Urgently Donate Funds to Disaster Areas Today

Principals, teachers, and students of all large, medium, and small schools in the city will begin a campaign to urgently donate funds to disaster areas today. The minimum standard for teachers is one yuan, college students four jiao, middle school students two jiao, and primary school students one jiao. With the mobilization of the entire city, the results should be more than 50,000 yuan. It is reported that the school authorities decided to complete the donation in the morning in order to facilitate the students' travel and avoid repeated donations, as the Boy Scouts will be conducting street fundraising today.

Military Training for High School Students in This City Will Be Conducted in a Centralized Training Next Year

Training for Three Months from April to July

It is Said That the Training Site May Be the Shanghai Road Racecourse

The Ministry of Education and the Training Supervision Department have decided that from next year, all military training students in senior high schools and equivalent schools in all provinces and cities must undergo three months of centralized training before the summer vacation. In this city, the National Military Training Committee is responsible for the preparations. The period will run from April to July next year. However, there are more than 70 schools in this city that implement military training, and the number of military training students exceeds several thousand. It is difficult to find a suitable training venue for a while. During this year's summer military training, the location also encountered difficulties, so the method of separate training by each school in stages was adopted. However, the centralized training to be held next year cannot adopt this method. It is said that it is planned to borrow the Shanghai Racecourse as a training venue. The location of the racecourse is large and quite suitable. Once the negotiation is completed, it can be decided. All military training students from all schools must participate in this training. Students who have received military training and obtained a team certificate during this year's summer training will receive preferential treatment when participating in the centralized training next year. As for schools above the specialized level who did not participate in the summer military training this year, they will still need to make up for the training next year.

The champions of the two groups received large silver cups, and the second, third, and sixth place winners received small silver cups. All team members were given commemorative badges. The ceremony ended at 11:00 AM with music and dismissal.
